-    SWIT_BswRslvrOffsHndlr_RslvrOffsManagement_EndHook();

+   EMM_ModeType emm_mode;
+
+   emm_mode = Rte_Mode_BswRslvrOffsHndlr_BswRslvrOffsHndlrReqEmmMode_EmmMode();/*PRQA S 4442*/

+   {
+      case RODA:
+      {

+            BswRslvrOff_NvmWrPre_Cn++;

+         break;
+      }
+      case UDS:
+      {

+         {
+            BswRslvrOffHndlr_NvmHnd();
+         }

+         break;

+/******************************************************************************
+ * Name:           BswRslvrOffsHndlr_Main
+ * Description:    State machine for Bsw Resolver Offset handler
+ * TraceAbility    100kW-49647
+ *****************************************************************************/
+STATIC void BswRslvrOffHndlr_CommonCalib(BswRslvrNvmHndType type)
+{
+   CalibMode = type;
+
+   switch( SftyC2cData.StsCalibSfty )
+   {
+      case BSWRSLVR_STSFTYCLIB_CPMLETE:
+      {
+         BswRslvrOff_CalibSt_Cn = 0;/*PRQA S 1290*/
+         NvmHndlrRslvrOffs.RslvrOffs = SftyC2cData.RslvrOffsNvm.RslvrOffs;
+         NvmHndlrRslvrOffs.RslvrOffsChks = SftyC2cData.RslvrOffsNvm.RslvrOffsChks;
+         NvmHndlrRslvrOffs.Pattern = SftyC2cData.RslvrOffsNvm.Pattern;
+         (void)Rte_Write_BswRslvrOffsHndlr_BswRslvrOffsHndlr_RslvrOffsUds_RslvrOffsVal(NvmHndlrRslvrOffs.RslvrOffs);
+
+         BswRslvrOffHndlr_NvmHndPre(CalibMode);
+
+         break;
+      }
+      case BSWRSLVR_STSFTYCLIB_PROGRESS:
+      {
+         BswRslvrOff_CalibSt_Cn = 0;/*PRQA S 1290*/
+
+         break;
+      }
+      case BSWRSLVR_STSFTYCLIB_FAILED:
+      {
+         BswRslvrOff_CalibSt_Cn = 0;/*PRQA S 1290*/
+
+         if( BswErrDebFctInhbnSts.B.FctIdRslvrOffsFlt )/*PRQA S 3344*/
+         {
+            ReqCalibSftyType = REQ_NONE;
+            BswC2cData.ReqCalibSfty = REQ_CALIB_SFTY_NONE;
+         }
+         else if( CalibMode == RODA )
+         {
+            ReqCalibSftyType = REQ_ONLINE_CAL;
+            BswC2cData.ReqCalibSfty = REQ_CALIB_SFTY_RSLVR_OFFS_ONLINE_CAL;
+         }
+         else if( CalibMode == UDS )
+         {
+            ReqCalibSftyType = REQ_VERIFICATION_UDS;
+            BswC2cData.ReqCalibSfty = REQ_CALIB_SFTY_RSLVR_OFFS_VERIFICATION_UDS;
+         }
+         else
+         {
+            /* Do nothing. */
+         }
+
+         break;
+      }
+      case BSWRSLVR_STSFTYCLIB_INACTIVE:
+      {
+         BswRslvrOff_CalibSt_Cn++;
+
+         if( (BSWRSLVR_UDSCALIB_THRESHOLD >= BswRslvrOff_CalibSt_Cn) && (CalibMode == UDS) )
+         {
+            /* Do nothing; */
+         }
+         else if( (BSWRSLVR_RODACALIB_THRESHOLD >= BswRslvrOff_CalibSt_Cn) && (CalibMode == RODA) )
+         {
+            /* Do nothing. */
+         }
+         else
+         {
+            BswRslvrOff_RodaCalibSt_TO = TRUE;
+            ReqCalibSftyType = REQ_NONE;
+            BswC2cData.ReqCalibSfty = REQ_CALIB_SFTY_NONE;
+         }
+
+         break;
+      }
+      default:
+      {
+         /* Do nothing. */
+         break;
+      }
+   }
+}
+
+/******************************************************************************
+ * Name:           BswRslvrOffHndlr_Nvm_Veri
+ * Description:    State machine for Bsw Resolver Offset handler
+ * TraceAbility    100kW-49646
+ *****************************************************************************/
+STATIC void BswRslvrOffHndlr_Nvm_Veri(void)
+{
+   switch( SftyC2cData.RslvrOffsVld )
+   {
+      case BSWRSLVR_VID_UNDETERMINED:
+      {
+         BswRslvrOff_NvmVeri_Cn++;
+
+         if( BSWRSLVR_NVMVERI_THRESHOLD >= BswRslvrOff_NvmVeri_Cn )
+         {
+            /* Do nothing; */
+         }
+         else
+         {
+            BswRslvrOff_NvmVeri_TO = TRUE;
+            ReqCalibSftyType = REQ_NONE;
+            BswC2cData.ReqCalibSfty = REQ_CALIB_SFTY_NONE;
+         }
+
+         break;
+      }
+      case BSWRSLVR_VID_INVALID:
+      {
+         if( BswErrDebFctInhbnSts.B.FctIdRslvrOffsInitFlt )/*PRQA S 3344*/
+         {
+            ReqCalibSftyType = REQ_ONLINE_CAL;
+            BswC2cData.ReqCalibSfty = REQ_CALIB_SFTY_RSLVR_OFFS_ONLINE_CAL;
+            (void)Rte_Write_BswRslvrOffsHndlr_BswRslvrOffsHndlr_RslvrOffsVldtInit_boolean(TRUE);
+         }
+         else
+         {
+            ReqCalibSftyType = REQ_VERIFICATION_NVM;
+            BswC2cData.ReqCalibSfty = REQ_CALIB_SFTY_RSLVR_OFFS_VERIFICATION_NVM;
+         }
+
+         break;
+      }
+      case BSWRSLVR_VID_VALID:
+      {
+         ReqCalibSftyType = REQ_NONE;
+         BswC2cData.ReqCalibSfty = REQ_CALIB_SFTY_NONE;
+         (void)Rte_Write_BswRslvrOffsHndlr_BswRslvrOffsHndlr_RslvrOffsVldtInit_boolean(FALSE);
+         (void)Rte_Write_BswRslvrOffsHndlr_BswRslvrOffsHndlr_RslvrOffsUds_RslvrOffsVal(NvmHndlrRslvrOffs.RslvrOffs);
+         break;
+      }
+      default:
+      {
+         /* Do nothing. */
+         break;
+      }
+   }
+
+}
+
+/******************************************************************************
+ * Name:           BswRslvrOffsHndlr_Main
+ * Description:    State machine for Bsw Resolver Offset handler
+ * TraceAbility    100kW-49645
+ *****************************************************************************/
+STATIC void BswRslvrOffHndlr_Online_Cal(void)
+{
+   if( BSWRSLVR_RODACALIB_THRESHOLD > BswRslvrOff_CalibSt_Cn )
+   {
+      BswRslvrOffHndlr_CommonCalib(RODA);
+   }
+   else
+   {
+      BswRslvrOff_CalibSt_Cn = 0;/*PRQA S 1290*/
+      BswRslvrOff_RodaCalibSt_TO = TRUE;
+      ReqCalibSftyType = REQ_NONE;
+      BswC2cData.ReqCalibSfty = REQ_CALIB_SFTY_NONE;
+   }
+
 }
 
+/******************************************************************************
+ * Name:           BswRslvrOffsHndlr_Main
+ * Description:    State machine for Bsw Resolver Offset handler
+ * TraceAbility    100kW-49644
+ *****************************************************************************/
+STATIC void BswRslvrOffHndlr_Nvm_PreWr(void)
+{
+   if( BswRslvrOff_NvmWrPre_Cn >= BSWRSLVR_NVMWRPRE_THRESHOLD )
+   {
+      ReqCalibSftyType = REQ_NONE;
+      BswC2cData.ReqCalibSfty = REQ_CALIB_SFTY_NONE;
+      BswRslvrOff_NvmWrPre_TO = TRUE;
+   }
+   else
+   {
+      BswRslvrOffHndlr_NvmHndPre(CalibMode);
+   }
+
+}

+STATIC void BswRslvrOffHndlr_Nvm_Wr(void)
+{
+   BswRslvrOffHndlr_NvmHnd();
+}

+        break;
+      }
+      case REQ_NVM_WRITE:
+      {
+         BswRslvrOffHndlr_Nvm_Wr();
+        break;
+      }
+      case REQ_NVM_WAIT:
+      {
+         BswRslvrOffHndlr_Nvm_Wait();
+        break;
+      }
+      case REQ_NONE:
+      {
+         BswRslvrOffHndlr_None();
+        break;
+      }
+      case REQ_VERIFICATION_UDS:
+      {
+         BswRslvrOffHndlr_Uds_Veri();
+        break;
+      }
+      default:
+      {
+         /* Do nothing. */
+         break;
+      }
+
+   }
